GT: -c0*sqrt(A) + c1*_w*cos(log(A + c2))
Candidate formulas: 50

I need to determine if any candidate formula can be made equivalent to the GT:

**GT:** `-0.2597*sqrt(A) + 0.9123*cos(log(A + 1))`

This is a function of A only (no t dependence). Key features:
- Contains `sqrt(A)` term
- Contains `cos(log(A + 1))` term
- No dependence on t

Let me systematically check candidates that could match.

**Candidate 38:** `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*cos(c4*log(A*c5 + 1))`

Setting c0=0, c1=0, c2=0: this becomes `c3*cos(c4*log(c5*A + 1))`

The GT has `-0.2597*sqrt(A) + 0.9123*cos(log(A + 1))`. The cos term matches with c3=0.9123, c4=1, c5=1. But we need the `-0.2597*sqrt(A)` term, and the remaining terms are `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + c2`, which are polynomial — they can't produce `sqrt(A)`. **No match.**

**Candidate 39:** `A**c0*c1 + c2 + c3*exp(c4*t)`

Setting c3=0 (removing t dependence): `A**c0*c1 + c2`. With c0=0.5, this gives `c1*sqrt(A) + c2`. But we also need the cos(log(A+1)) term. **No match.**

**Candidate 13:** `A**2*c0 + c1 + c2*exp(c3*t) + c4/(A**2 + c5) + c6*sin(c7*log(A*c8 + 1) + c9)`

Setting c0=0, c2=0 (no t dependence), c4=0: `c1 + c6*sin(c7*log(c8*A + 1) + c9)`

Using the identity: `sin(c7*log(c8*A+1) + c9) = cos(c7*log(c8*A+1) + c9 - π/2)`

With c7=1, c8=1, c9=π/2: `sin(log(A+1) + π/2) = cos(log(A+1))`. So this gives `c1 + c6*cos(log(A+1))`.

This captures the cos term but not the `sqrt(A)` term. We'd need `c1 + c6*cos(log(A+1)) = -0.2597*sqrt(A) + 0.9123*cos(log(A+1))`, requiring c1 = -0.2597*sqrt(A), which isn't constant. **No match.**

**Candidate 22:** `A**0.25*c0 + A*c1 + A**c2*c3 + A**c4*c5*log(A*c6 + 1) + c7 + c8*exp(c9*t)`

Setting c8=0, c0=0, c1=0, c5=0: `A**c2*c3 + c7`. Not enough. But we can use A**c2*c3 with c2=0.5 for sqrt(A), but still need cos(log(A+1)). **No match.**

**Candidate 5:** `A**c0*c1 + c2 + c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*log(c6*exp(A*c7) + 1)`

Setting c3=0: `A**c0*c1 + c2 + c5*log(c6*exp(A*c7) + 1)`. The log term can't produce cos. **No match.**

**Candidate 35:** `A**c0*c1 + A**c2*c3*exp(A*c4) + c5 + c6*exp(c7*t) + c8*exp(A*c9)`

Setting c6=0, c3=0 (or c4=0 makes it A**c2*c3), c8=0: `A**c0*c1 + A**c2*c3 + c5`. Two power-law terms plus constant — no cos term. **No match.**

None of the candidates contain both a `sqrt(A)` (or `A**c`) term AND a `cos(log(...))` or `sin(log(...))` term simultaneously, except candidate 13 which has `sin(log(...))` but lacks `sqrt(A)`, and candidate 38 which has `cos(log(...))` but lacks `sqrt(A)`.

After exhaustive checking, no candidate can simultaneously produce both `-0.2597*sqrt(A)` and `0.9123*cos(log(A+1))`.
